behavior find_food_vegetable_2041_around_fridge_289(food_vegetable:item):
    goal: not unknown(food_vegetable)
    body:
        assert is_food_vegetable(food_vegetable)
        bind fridge_instance:item where:
            is_fridge(fridge_instance) and id[fridge_instance]==289
        achieve close_char(char,fridge_instance)
        if can_open(fridge_instance):
            achieve_once open(fridge_instance)
            exp(food_vegetable,fridge_instance)
        else:
            exp(food_vegetable,fridge_instance)
    eff:
        unknown[food_vegetable]=False
        close[food_vegetable,fridge_instance]=True
        close[fridge_instance,food_vegetable]=True

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_all_in_fridge_to_trashcan(fridge:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select the fridge from which the items need to be thrown away

        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select a trashcan to throw the items into

        throw_all_in_fridge_to_trashcan(fridge, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_in_trash(items:item, trashcan:item): 
    body:
        achieve_once inside(items, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)

        foreach items: item:
            if inside(items, fridge):
                throw_in_trash(items, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

Goal representation from planning.py

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation

behavior throw_item_in_trash(item:item, trash_can:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trash_can)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        
        bind trash_can: item where:
            is_trashcan(trash_can)

        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_item_in_trash(item, trash_can)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_to_trash(item: item, trashcan: item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select the fridge
        
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select a trashcan
        
        foreach item: item:
            # Iterate over all items in the fridge
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_to_trash(item, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_into_trashcan(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select the fridge
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select the trashcan
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_into_trashcan(item, trashcan)


#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_items_to_trash(item: item, fridge: item, trashcan: item):
    body:
        # Ensure the fridge is open to take items out
        achieve_once open(fridge)
        
        # Place each item inside the trashcan
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)
        
behavior __goal__():
    body:
        # Bind fridge and trashcan to respective items
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        
        # Iterate over all items in the fridge
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                # Throw each item in the fridge into the trashcan
                throw_items_to_trash(item, fridge, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_in_trash(fridge_item:item, trashcan:item): 
    body:
        achieve_once inside(fridge_item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
            
        foreach fridge_item: item:
            if inside(fridge_item, fridge):
                throw_in_trash(fridge_item, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_all_fridge_items_to_trashcan(fridge:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve open(fridge)
        # Open the fridge to access the items inside
        foreach item: item:
            # Iterate over each item inside the fridge
            if inside(item, fridge):
                achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)
                # Throw the item into the trash can

behavior close_the_fridge_door(fridge:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(fridge)
        # Close the fridge door

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select the fridge
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select the trash can
        throw_all_fridge_items_to_trashcan(fridge, trashcan)
        # Throw all items in the fridge to the trash can
        close_the_fridge_door(fridge)
        # Close the fridge door afterwards

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_all_items_in_trashcan(fridge:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        throw_all_items_in_trashcan(fridge, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

Goal representation from planning.py

#goal_representation
 
behavior open_fridge(fridge:item):
    body:
        achieve_once open(fridge)

behavior throw_items_in_trash(fridge:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge) and is_food(item):
                achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior close_fridge(fridge:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(fridge)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)

        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)

        open_fridge(fridge)
        throw_items_in_trash(fridge, trashcan)
        close_fridge(fridge)

#goal_representation_end
